[CREATURE:BIRD_CROW]
	[DESCRIPTION:A small black bird that feeds on carrion.  It is social, very intelligent and knows how to use tools.]
	[NAME:crow:crows:crow]
	[CASTE_NAME:crow:crows:crow]
	[GENERAL_CHILD_NAME:crow hatchling:crow hatchlings]
	[CREATURE_TILE:249][COLOR:0:0:1]
	[PETVALUE:10][NATURAL][PET]
	[BIOME:GRASSLAND_TEMPERATE]
	[BIOME:SAVANNA_TEMPERATE]
	[BIOME:SHRUBLAND_TEMPERATE]
	[BIOME:FOREST_TAIGA]

	[BIOME:ANY_TEMPERATE_WETLAND]
	[VERMIN_GROUNDER][FREQUENCY:100]
	[POPULATION_NUMBER:250:500]
	[SMALL_REMAINS]
	[BENIGN][FLIER]
	[CHILD:1]
	[DIURNAL]
	[HOMEOTHERM:10071]

	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:STANDARD_SWIMMING_GAITS:9000:8900:8825:8775:9500:9900] 1 kph, NO DATA
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:STANDARD_CRAWLING_GAITS:9000:8900:8825:8775:9500:9900] 1 kph, NO DATA
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:STANDARD_CLIMBING_GAITS:9000:8900:8825:8775:9500:9900] 1 kph, NO DATA
	[STANCE_CLIMBER][NATURAL_SKILL:CLIMBING:15]
	[PREFSTRING:intelligence]
	[BODY:HUMANOID_ARMLESS_NECK:2WINGS:2EYES:2LUNGS:HEART:GUTS:ORGANS:GIZZARD:HUMANOID_JOINTS:THROAT:NECK:SPINE:BRAIN:SKULL:4TOES:BEAK:RIBCAGE]
	[BODY_DETAIL_PLAN:STANDARD_SMALL_MATERIALS]{:STANDARD_MATERIALS  Revision: too small to yield leather.}
		[REMOVE_MATERIAL:HAIR]
		[USE_MATERIAL_TEMPLATE:FEATHER:FEATHER_TEMPLATE]
	[BODY_DETAIL_PLAN:STANDARD_TISSUES]
		[REMOVE_TISSUE:HAIR]
		[USE_TISSUE_TEMPLATE:FEATHER:FEATHER_TEMPLATE]
	[BODY_DETAIL_PLAN:VERTEBRATE_TISSUE_LAYERS:SKIN:FAT:MUSCLE:BONE:CARTILAGE]
	[BODY_DETAIL_PLAN:BODY_FEATHER_TISSUE_LAYERS:FEATHER]
	[USE_MATERIAL_TEMPLATE:TALON:NAIL_TEMPLATE]
	[USE_TISSUE_TEMPLATE:TALON:TALON_TEMPLATE]
	[TISSUE_LAYER:BY_CATEGORY:TOE:TALON:FRONT]
	[BODY_DETAIL_PLAN:EGG_MATERIALS]
	[SELECT_TISSUE_LAYER:HEART:BY_CATEGORY:HEART]
	 [PLUS_TISSUE_LAYER:SKIN:BY_CATEGORY:THROAT]
		[TL_MAJOR_ARTERIES]
	[BODY_DETAIL_PLAN:STANDARD_HEAD_POSITIONS]
	[BODY_DETAIL_PLAN:HUMANOID_RIBCAGE_POSITIONS]

	[TENDONS:LOCAL_CREATURE_MAT:SINEW:200]
	[LIGAMENTS:LOCAL_CREATURE_MAT:SINEW:200]
	[HAS_NERVES]
	[USE_MATERIAL_TEMPLATE:BLOOD:BLOOD_TEMPLATE]
	[BLOOD:LOCAL_CREATURE_MAT:BLOOD:LIQUID]
	[CREATURE_CLASS:GENERAL_POISON]
	[GETS_WOUND_INFECTIONS]
	[GETS_INFECTIONS_FROM_ROT]
	[USE_MATERIAL_TEMPLATE:PUS:PUS_TEMPLATE]
	[PUS:LOCAL_CREATURE_MAT:PUS:LIQUID]
	[BODY_SIZE:0:0:20]
	[BODY_SIZE:1:0:500]
	[BODY_APPEARANCE_MODIFIER:LENGTH:90:95:98:100:102:105:110]
	[BODY_APPEARANCE_MODIFIER:HEIGHT:90:95:98:100:102:105:110]
	[BODY_APPEARANCE_MODIFIER:BROADNESS:90:95:98:100:102:105:110]
	[MAXAGE:10:15]
	[ATTACK:BITE:BODYPART:BY_CATEGORY:BEAK]
		[ATTACK_SKILL:BITE]

		[ATTACK_PENETRATION_PERC:100]

		[ATTACK_PREPARE_AND_RECOVER:3:3]
		[ATTACK_PRIORITY:MAIN]
		[ATTACK_FLAG_CANLATCH]
	[ATTACK:SCRATCH:CHILD_TISSUE_LAYER_GROUP:BY_TYPE:STANCE:BY_CATEGORY:ALL:TALON]
		[ATTACK_SKILL:STANCE_STRIKE]
		[ATTACK_VERB:snatch at:snatches at]
		[ATTACK_CONTACT_PERC:100]
		[ATTACK_PENETRATION_PERC:100]
		[ATTACK_FLAG_EDGE]
		[ATTACK_PREPARE_AND_RECOVER:3:3]
		[ATTACK_PRIORITY:SECOND]
		[ATTACK_FLAG_WITH]
		[ATTACK_FLAG_BAD_MULTIATTACK]
	[CASTE:FEMALE]
		[FEMALE]
		[DESCRIPTION:A small, carrion-feeding bird with black, almost glossy feathers.  She's social, intelligent, and knows how to use tools.  She can also be noisy, especially when joined by flocks of her kind.]{+}
		[LAYS_EGGS]
			[EGG_MATERIAL:LOCAL_CREATURE_MAT:EGGSHELL:SOLID]
			[EGG_MATERIAL:LOCAL_CREATURE_MAT:EGG_WHITE:LIQUID]
			[EGG_MATERIAL:LOCAL_CREATURE_MAT:EGG_YOLK:LIQUID]
			[EGG_SIZE:21]
			[CLUTCH_SIZE:4:6]
	[CASTE:MALE]
		[MALE]
		[DESCRIPTION:A small, carrion-feeding bird with black, almost glossy feathers.  He's social, intelligent, and knows how to use tools.  He can also be noisy, especially when joined by flocks of his kind.]{+}
	[SELECT_CASTE:ALL]
		[SET_TL_GROUP:BY_CATEGORY:ALL:FEATHER]
			[TL_COLOR_MODIFIER:BLACK:1]
				[TLCM_NOUN:feathers:PLURAL]
		[SET_TL_GROUP:BY_CATEGORY:BEAK:BONE]{+  Revision: describe crow beaks as black.}
			[TL_COLOR_MODIFIER:BLACK:1]
				[TLCM_NOUN:beak:SINGULAR]
		[SET_TL_GROUP:BY_CATEGORY:ALL:SKIN]
	[TL_COLOR_MODIFIER:BROWN:1:BURNT_UMBER:1:CINNAMON:1:COPPER:1:DARK_BROWN:1:DARK_PEACH:1:DARK_TAN:1:ECRU:1:PALE_BROWN:1:PALE_CHESTNUT:1:PALE_PINK:1:PEACH:1:PINK:1:RAW_UMBER:1:SEPIA:1:TAN:1:TAUPE_PALE:1:TAUPE_SANDY:1]
				[TLCM_NOUN:skin:SINGULAR]
		[SET_TL_GROUP:BY_CATEGORY:EYE:EYE]
			[TL_COLOR_MODIFIER:BLACK:1]
				[TLCM_NOUN:eyes:PLURAL]

[CREATURE:CROW_MAN]
	[COPY_TAGS_FROM:BIRD_CROW]
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:ANIMAL_PERSON]
	[GO_TO_END]
	[SELECT_CASTE:MALE]
		[CASTE_NAME:crow man:crow men:crow man]
		[DESCRIPTION:A small, foreboding harpy with winged arms and the head of a crow.  His black, glossy feathers are longer around his neck, forming a scarf.  He has a shadowy appearance save for where his feathers thin, showing skin.  His body is unusually light.  He doesn't care that he's naked.]{+}
	[SELECT_CASTE:FEMALE]
		[CASTE_NAME:crow woman:crow women:crow woman]
		[DESCRIPTION:A small, foreboding harpy with winged arms and the head of a crow.  Her black, glossy feathers are longer around her neck, forming a scarf.  She has a shadowy appearance save for where her feathers thin, showing skin.  Her body is unusually light.  She doesn't care that she's naked.]{+}
	[SELECT_CASTE:ALL]
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:PUNCH_ATTACK]
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:TALON_KICK_ATTACK]{:KICK_ATTACK  Revision: combined the talon scratch and kick attacks.}
	{APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:TALON_SCRATCH_ATTACK}
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:BEAK_BITE_ATTACK]
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:STANDARD_BIPED_GAITS:900:750:600:439:1900:2900] 20 kph
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:STANDARD_FLYING_GAITS:900:691:482:251:1900:2900] 35 kph
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:STANDARD_CLIMBING_GAITS:2990:2257:1525:731:4300:6100] 12 kph
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:STANDARD_SWIMMING_GAITS:2990:2257:1525:731:4300:6100] 12 kph
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:STANDARD_CRAWLING_GAITS:2990:2257:1525:731:4300:6100] 12 kph
	[GO_TO_START]
	[NAME:crow man:crow men:crow man]
	[DESCRIPTION:A small person with the head and wings of a crow.]
	[POPULATION_NUMBER:5:10]
	[CLUSTER_NUMBER:5:10]
	[MAXAGE:60:80]
	[CREATURE_TILE:'c']
	[COLOR:0:0:1]
	[SOUND:ALERT:100:10000:VOCALIZATION:caw angrily:caws angrily:angry cawing]{+  Revision: vocalizations help the world feel alive.}
	[SOUND:PEACEFUL_INTERMITTENT:100:10000:VOCALIZATION:caw:caws:distant cawing]{+}
	[NATURAL_SKILL:DODGING:3]{+  Revision: help crow people feel more unique.}
	[NATURAL_SKILL:SNEAK:3]{+  Revision: crows are shifty.}
	[PHYS_ATT_RANGE:AGILITY:450:950:1150:1250:1350:1550:2250]+{+}

[CREATURE:GIANT_CROW]
	[COPY_TAGS_FROM:BIRD_CROW]
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:GIANT]
	[CV_REMOVE_TAG:CHANGE_BODY_SIZE_PERC]
	[APPLY_CURRENT_CREATURE_VARIATION]
	[GO_TO_END]
	[SELECT_CASTE:FEMALE]
		[DESCRIPTION:An inquisitive bird-like monster with black, almost glossy feathers and an ominous, echoing call.  She scavenges for food and carrion, tearing flesh with her long beak.]{+}
	[SELECT_CASTE:MALE]
		[DESCRIPTION:An inquisitive bird-like monster with black, almost glossy feathers and an ominous, echoing call.  He scavenges for food and carrion, tearing flesh with his long beak.]{+}
	[SELECT_CASTE:ALL]
	[CHANGE_BODY_SIZE_PERC:40700]
	[GO_TO_START]
	[NAME:giant crow:giant crows:giant crow]
	[CASTE_NAME:giant crow:giant crows:giant crow]
	[GENERAL_CHILD_NAME:giant crow hatchling:giant crow hatchlings]
	[DESCRIPTION:A large bird-like monster, even more deadly when found in groups.]
	[POPULATION_NUMBER:30:50]
	[CLUSTER_NUMBER:5:10]
	[CREATURE_TILE:'C']
	[COLOR:0:0:1]
	[PET_EXOTIC]
	[PETVALUE:500]
	[MOUNT_EXOTIC]
	[SOUND:ALERT:100:10000:VOCALIZATION:caw angrily:caws angrily:angry cawing]{+  Revision: vocalizations help the world feel alive.}
	[SOUND:PEACEFUL_INTERMITTENT:100:10000:VOCALIZATION:caw:caws:distant cawing]{+}
	[GO_TO_END]
